[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA libFuzzer run under Jazzer reported a timeout after ~[0m[1;36m28[0m[39m s while exercising a PDF [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtext-extraction fuzz target. The main thread is stuck repeatedly in the native [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcallback `TraceDataFlowNativeCallbacks.traceConstCmpInt`, invoked from [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Type1Parser.parseBinary` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mApache FontBox[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. There is no crash or exception—rather, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe fuzzer target failed to complete within the allotted time.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzer invocation did not finish—libFuzzer declared a timeout. This [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrepresents a hang or excessive execution time [0m[1;39m([0m[39ma potential denial-of-service [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mscenario[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, not a memory safety crash or exception.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- What the issue is  [0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  When processing a crafted input, the PDF text-extraction harness [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`PDFExtractTextFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m invokes PDFBox’s [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mPDFTextStripper.getText[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`. During font parsing, the `Type1Parser.parseBinary` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmethod enters a tight loop under Jazzer’s data-flow tracing [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`traceConstCmpInt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand never returns within the fuzzer’s timeout window.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Observations and findings  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The JVM thread dump shows the “main” thread continuously RUNNABLE in the native[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcallback at `TraceDataFlowNativeCallbacks.traceConstCmpInt`.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The call stack frames from PDFBox indicate the path:  [0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    – `Type1Parser.parseBinary` → `Type1Parser.parse` → `Type1Font.createWithPFB` →[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`PDType1Font.<init>` → `PDFontFactory.createFont` → `PDResources.getFont` → [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SetFontAndSize.process` → `PDFStreamEngine.process*` → `PDFTextStripper.getText` →[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzer harness.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • No other threads are blocked or throwing exceptions—most are JVM housekeeping [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mor GC threads.[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas to investigate  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To understand why parsing a Type [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m font can hang indefinitely under fuzzing [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minstrumentation, review:  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `org.apache.fontbox.type1.Type1Parser.parseBinary` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mespecially around line [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m640[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. The sequence of calls in PDFBox that lead into `Type1Parser` [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g. [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`Type1Font.createWithPFB`, `PDType1Font`, `PDFontFactory`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. The fuzzer harness entry point [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PDFExtractTextFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhow it feeds input into `PDFTextStripper`.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Jazzer’s native callback implementation [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`TraceDataFlowNativeCallbacks.traceConstCmpInt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, to gauge overhead and potential [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minteraction with tight loops in the parser.[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
